like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . the majority of side effects listed below is defined using the following convention : very common ( affects more than 1 user in 10 ) common ( affects 1 to 10 users in 100 ) rare ( affects 1 to 10 users in 1 , 000 ) rare ( affects 1 to 10 users in 10 , 000 ) very rare ( affects 1 to 10 users in 10 , 000 ) very rare ( affects less than 1 user in 10 , 000 ) not known ( frequency cannot be estimated from the available data ) side effects reported with wilzin are : very common ( affects more than 1 user in 10 ) common ( affects 1 to 10 users in 100 ) uncommon ( affects 1 to 10 users in 1 , 000 ) rare ( affects 1 to 10 users in 10 , 000 ) very rare ( affects less than 1 user in 10 , 000 ) not known ( frequency cannot be estimated from the available data ) reporting of side effects if you get any side effects , talk to your doctor or pharmacist . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet . you can also report side effects directly via the national reporting system listed in appendix v . by reporting side effects you can help provide more information on the safety of this medicine .

like all medicines , this vaccine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . these side effects may happen with the use of mvabea . the most frequently reported side effects are pain , swelling and redness where the injection is given . these side effects usually disappear within 1 - 2 days without treatment . if these side effects become severe , please tell your doctor or pharmacist . very common ( may affect more than 1 in 10 people ): pain , swelling and redness where the injection is given . common ( may affect up to 1 in 10 people ): warmth , swelling where the injection is given itching where the injection is given itching , pain , swelling and redness where the injection is given 17 than 39 . common ( may affect up to 1 in 10 people ): redness and swelling where the injection is given itching where the injection is given itching , pain , swelling , warmth and redness where the injection is given 17 than 39 . uncommon ( may affect up to 1 in 100 people ): swelling or non - cancerous sores in your skin ( redness and itching ) where the injection is given . reporting of side effects if you get any side effects , talk to your doctor or pharmacist . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet . you can also report side effects directly via the national reporting system listed in appendix v . by reporting side effects you can help provide more information on the safety of this medicine .
